<div id="review_1510792226" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1510792226" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388694025p2/3344685.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1510792226?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/3344685-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780356503950" href="/book/show/21090536-a-memory-of-light">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=books-i-own-kindle">books-i-own-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3344685-sarah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1510792226" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3997248973150809886">I still can't quite believe that the epic Wheel of Time series is actually over! 15 books (don't forget the prologue!), 12,097 pages and over a year of reading (I read one book a month with a group of friends) and it's done. I actually put off reading <b>A Memory of Light</b> because I didn't want to reach the end but I'm so glad it went out on a high note. This series is absolutely huge and I was nervous about making the commitment to it last year but I have really enjoyed the journey that <b>Robert Jord</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3997248973150809886" style="display:none">I still can't quite believe that the epic Wheel of Time series is actually over! 15 books (don't forget the prologue!), 12,097 pages and over a year of reading (I read one book a month with a group of friends) and it's done. I actually put off reading <b>A Memory of Light</b> because I didn't want to reach the end but I'm so glad it went out on a high note. This series is absolutely huge and I was nervous about making the commitment to it last year but I have really enjoyed the journey that <b>Robert Jordan</b> and <b>Brandon Sanderson</b> have taken us on, and I can see why this is considered a classic.<br /><br />I'm running out of words to use in praise of this series, just go back and read any of my other 14 reviews and it'll quickly become clear how much I've loved this world though. The characters have alternated between infuriating and amazing but the world is just so huge and detailed that it was very easy to get lost in. There have been a lot of highs and lows along the way but that is only to be expected in something so huge and the last four books have probably been my favourites in the whole series.<br /><br />I'm not really going to say too much about the final instalment other than to confirm that it was a worthy addition to the series. There is just so much going on in this book, so many different plot threads that all needed to be tied together, so many characters who needed to get their final moments of glory, enemies to be destroyed and friendships to be celebrated. There were moments that I celebrated and others that broke my heart but overall I couldn't have been more happy with the ending. Is it perfect? Probably not but it came pretty close and overall this is a series I think every fantasy fan should read. I'm sad to say goodbye to these characters and if I'm honest I'm a little disappointed we didn't get an epilogue to show how our favourites are doing a few years down the line but I think we were given just enough that we can use our imagination for the rest.<br /><br />I'm sad that <b>Robert Jordan</b> didn't get the chance to finish his epic masterpiece but I'm thankful that <b>Brandon Sanderson</b> was able to do such a brilliant job of the final few books and I'm glad fans weren't left with a million unanswered questions.<br /><br />_________________<br /><br />Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/17825176-a-memory-of-light" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies, Books &amp; Baubles</a> starting <b>1st February 2017</b><br /><br />(I actually put of starting this for so long that I missed the group read entirely LOL)</span>
  <a data-text-id="3997248973150809886" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1464625616" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1464625616" />
    <a title="Sotiris Karaiskos" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18940246-sotiris-karaiskos"><img alt="Sotiris Karaiskos" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1407195235p2/18940246.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1464625616?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sotiris Karaiskos" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sotiris Karaiskos" href="/user/show/18940246-sotiris-karaiskos">Sotiris Karaiskos</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/17225466-a-memory-of-light">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18940246-sotiris-karaiskos?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18940246-sotiris-karaiskos?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18940246-sotiris-karaiskos?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1464625616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7322556460572532446">The end of a series of fantasy books is something very important, a bad end can ruin all the good impression created by the previous books, a good one can overturn any negative impression and put to the series in positive mark. In the case of this series, after 13 (and a half) amazing books the reader reaches an incredibly good ending, so you understand at what inconspicuous height the value of the whole work reaches. A last book that really makes it hard for me to describe it as it makes me fee</span>
  <span id="freeText7322556460572532446" style="display:none">The end of a series of fantasy books is something very important, a bad end can ruin all the good impression created by the previous books, a good one can overturn any negative impression and put to the series in positive mark. In the case of this series, after 13 (and a half) amazing books the reader reaches an incredibly good ending, so you understand at what inconspicuous height the value of the whole work reaches. A last book that really makes it hard for me to describe it as it makes me feel like the poet who tries to find the right words to add to his poem to make the greatest impression but can not do it. However, I have to make an effort.<br /><br />The subject of the book is, of course, is the grand final battle, where the powers of the Dark One make their great assault on world domination, and the forces of light throw their last dice for victory. The way the author describes it is more than staggering, managing to put us in its heart, to feel its brutality, to find ourselves next to every act of heroism, every attack, every sacrifice for the general good. But what makes this description stand out is not the action but the author's insistence on the thoughts and feelings of our heroes throughout this storm. Their anxiety, their fear of defeat, the alternation between hope and despair, their inner struggle to find the power they need to overcome their limitations, the doubt about the correctness of their decisions, all this becomes our own, making our emotional engagement to be absolute. The culmination of this are the thoughts on the nature of evil, of the ideal world and of the reasons why all these people are fighting and are willing to sacrifice their lives, which also gives a philosophical dimension.<br /><br />With these we move from the beginning to the end of the book as the writer slowly builds the tension, leading us to the most exciting culminations that concentrate all the essence of everything we read in these books. Thus, reading this breathtaking pages, we live intense literary moments, while realising that nothing is random. In terms of character, each of the heroes that made us company from the beginning completes its evolution, doing what he or she was intended for, in some of the most interesting and moving scenes. In a series based on these characters this is very important and gives us a reason to ponder their entire course until their happy or sad end.<br /><br />After all this, in the end, with the storm of images and emotions still in the mind and the intensity of the battle almost creating physical fatigue for the reader, we read the epilogue with a smile of satisfaction, not just for what we read in the last book but also for the whole series and for the emotions it offered us, confirming the greatness of this work. At this point, from the first reading, this series definitely won a place in my heart. And because there are no beginnings nor endings to the turning of the Wheel of Time all I have to do is soon to start again the journey from the beginning.<br /><br />ORIGINAL REVIEW<br /><br />I've just finished the reading of the last book of this series, it took me 2,5 months and I can tell that this was one of my best reading experiences. This series is an excellent example of high fantasy, strong rooted to Tolkien's work, with a fantasy world very well constructed and great descriptions of heroic deeds but I have found more than that in it. I think is more about characters. Robert Jordan is exploiting the huge size of this work to create and evolve excellent characters, making them so real that in the end we see them as real life friends (or foes). This is the real power of this series, making it not just books to pass time but complete emotional experiences.<br /><br /> Το τέλος μίας σειρά βιβλίων φαντασίας είναι κάτι πάρα πολύ σημαντικό, ένα κακό τέλος μπορεί να καταστρέψει όλη την καλή εντύπωση που έχει δημιουργηθεί από τα προηγούμενα βιβλία, ένα καλό μπορεί να ανατρέψει κάθε αρνητική εντύπωση και να βάλει στη σειρά θετικό πρόσημο. Στην περίπτωση αυτής της σειράς, μετά από 13 (και μισό) καταπληκτικά βιβλία ο αναγνώστης φτάνει σε ένα απίστευτα καλό τέλος, οπότε καταλαβαίνετε σε τι δυσθεώρητα ύψη φτάνει η αξία ολόκληρου του έργου. Ένα τελευταίο βιβλίο που πραγματικά είναι δύσκολο για εμένα να το περιγράψω καθώς με κάνει να αισθάνομαι σαν τον ποιητή που προσπαθεί να βρει τις κατάλληλες λέξεις να προσθέσει στο ποίημά του για να κάνει τη μέγιστη δυνατή εντύπωση αλλά δεν μπορεί να τα καταφέρει. Παρόλα αυτά πρέπει να κάνω μία προσπάθεια.<br /><br />Το θέμα του βιβλίου είναι φυσικά η μεγαλειώδης τελική μάχη, όπου οι δυνάμεις του σκοτεινού κάνουν τη μεγάλη τους επίθεση για την κυριαρχία του κόσμου και οι δυνάμεις του φωτός ρίχνουν την τελευταία τους ζάρια για τη νίκη. Ο τρόπος που ο συγγραφέας την περιγράφει είναι κάτι παραπάνω από συγκλονιστικός, καταφέρνοντας να μας βάλει στην καρδιά της, να μας κάνει να νιώσουμε τη βιαιότητα της, να βρεθούμε δίπλα σε κάθε πράξη ηρωισμού, σε κάθε επίθεση, σε κάθε θυσία για το γενικότερο καλό. Αυτό, όμως, που κάνει αυτή την περιγραφή να ξεχωρίζει δεν είναι η δράση αλλά η επιμονή του συγγραφέα στις σκέψεις και τα συναισθήματα των ηρώων μέσα σε όλη αυτή τη θύελλα. Η αγωνία τους, ο φόβος τους για την ήττα, η εναλλαγή ανάμεσα στην ελπίδα και την απελπισία, η εσωτερική τους μάχη για να βρουν τη δύναμη που χρειάζεται για να ξεπεράσουν τα όριά τους, η αμφιβολία για την ορθότητα των αποφάσεων τους, όλα αυτά γίνονται δικά μας κάνοντας την συναισθηματική μας εμπλοκή να είναι απόλυτη. Ως επιστέγασμα σε αυτό έρχονται και οι σκέψεις για την φύση του κακού, για τον ιδανικό κόσμο και γενικότερα για τους λόγους για τους οποίους όλοι αυτοί οι άνθρωποι πολεμάνε και είναι πρόθυμοι να θυσιάσουν τις ζωές τους, κάτι που δίνει και μία φιλοσοφική διάσταση. <br /><br />Με αυτά πορευόμαστε από την αρχή μέχρι το τέλος του βιβλίου καθώς ο συγγραφέας χτίζει σιγά-σιγά την ένταση οδηγώντας μας στις πιο συναρπαστικές κορυφώσεις που συμπυκνώνουν όλη την ουσία από όλα όσα διαβάσαμε σε αυτά τα βιβλία. Έτσι, διαβάζοντας με κομμένη την ανάσα, ζούμε έντονες λογοτεχνικές στιγμές, συνειδητοποιώντας παράλληλα ότι δεν υπάρχει τίποτα τυχαίο. Σε επίπεδο χαρακτήρων, κάθε ένας από τους ήρωες που μας έκαναν συντροφιά από την αρχή ολοκληρώνει την εξέλιξή του, κάνοντας αυτό για το οποίο προορίζονταν, σε κάποιες από τις πιο ενδιαφέρουσες και συγκινητικές σκηνές. Σε μία σειρά που βασίστηκε σε αυτούς τους χαρακτήρες αυτό είναι πολύ σημαντικό και μας δίνει την αφορμή να αναλογιστούμε όλη την πορεία τους μέχρι το χαρούμενο ή το λυπητερό τέλος της.<br /><br />Μετά από όλα αυτά, φτάνοντας στο τέλος, με τον καταιγισμό εικόνων και συναισθημάτων να είναι ακόμα στο μυαλό και την ένταση της μάχης σχεδόν να δημιουργεί σωματική κούραση στον αναγνώστη, διαβάζουμε τον επίλογο με ένα χαμόγελο ικανοποίησης, όχι μόνο για αυτά που διαβάσαμε στο τελευταίο βιβλίο αλλά και για ολόκληρη τη σειρά και για τις συγκινήσεις που μας προσέφερε, επιβεβαιώνοντας το μεγαλείο αυτού του έργου. Σε αυτό το σημείο, από την πρώτη ανάγνωση, αυτή η σειρά κέρδισε οριστικά μία θέση στην καρδιά μου Και επειδή δεν υπάρχει ούτε αρχή ούτε τέλος στο γύρισμα του Τροχού του Χρόνου το μόνο που μένει να κάνω είναι σύντομα να αρχίσω το ταξίδι από την αρχή.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7322556460572532446" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3204521509?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mike&#39;s Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mike&#39;s Book Reviews" href="/user/show/59173659-mike-s-book-reviews">Mike&#39;s Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3204521509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11809998480679478303">Full Video Reviews Here:<br/>Part I - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://youtu.be/N4YntXtOslQ'>https://youtu.be/N4YntXtOslQ</a><br/>Part II - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://youtu.be/emdpsNrashY'>https://youtu.be/emdpsNrashY</a><br/><br/>After 14 previous books, counting New Spring, beginning the final Wheel of Time book felt like something out of a dream. When I began this journey 13 months prior I was non-committal on finishing the series and said my only goal, really, was to stay ahead of the Amazon TV series. Exactly 400 days later, my journey through the Wheel came to an emotional close. <br/><br/>As I read the last 25 pages, it really </span>
  <span id="freeText11809998480679478303" style="display:none">Full Video Reviews Here:<br />Part I - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://youtu.be/N4YntXtOslQ">https://youtu.be/N4YntXtOslQ</a><br />Part II - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://youtu.be/emdpsNrashY">https://youtu.be/emdpsNrashY</a><br /><br />After 14 previous books, counting New Spring, beginning the final Wheel of Time book felt like something out of a dream. When I began this journey 13 months prior I was non-committal on finishing the series and said my only goal, really, was to stay ahead of the Amazon TV series. Exactly 400 days later, my journey through the Wheel came to an emotional close. <br /><br />As I read the last 25 pages, it really hit me that this was the end; there was no next book like I had the option of for the past year of my life. Stopping only to grab some Kleenex to wipe away the tears and blow my annoying nose, the journey came to a close so suddenly that I felt an overwhelming sense of loss. It wasn't that this particular book is heavily emotional as much as the realization of these friends I had made over the past year were going to be saying goodbye. That might be difficult for anyone to understand that hasn't made the trip through RandLand yet, but those who have understand exactly what I'm talking about.<br /><br />As for this actual book, it is an incredibly satisfying conclusion; even if it isn't perfect. For those who found the series too slow, you'll be happy you made it here as this final edition is a non-stop action thrill ride. The Last Battle, which has spent double-digit books building up to meets every expectation. There is loss, there is triumph, there are moments that will leave your jaw dropped and have you gasping out loud.<br /><br />In the end, there were many ups and downs in this run through the Wheel of Time. It's by no means perfect but it is a journey I think any fan of the genre should make. It's like getting bachelor's degree in Fantasy.<br /><br />400 days, 13 months, 15 books, 4.4 million words. 38 videos.<br /><br />I’ll always love and respect Wheel of Time for not only being an incredible journey, but the one that built Mike's Book Reviews into an actual thing. Started from the bottom now we here. Thank you, Mr. Jordan for creating this world and Mr. Sanderson for completing his work in a way I think he would have been proud of.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11809998480679478303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer583536957836487609">I'm still not sure how many of those stars are for sheer nostalgia - at least one? - but this was a hell of a wrap up for a 12 year journey. I started reading these books when I was 13, I am 25 now, and I can say there were times when I didn't see this ever ending. Through its ups (books 1-6), its downs (8-11), its not-bad-but-could-be-better (7, 12) this has remained a big force in my fantasy reading. Forgive me for this pun, but there will be a <i>void</i> where The Wheel of Time once stood. <br/><br/>Favorite</span>
  <span id="freeText583536957836487609" style="display:none">I'm still not sure how many of those stars are for sheer nostalgia - at least one? - but this was a hell of a wrap up for a 12 year journey. I started reading these books when I was 13, I am 25 now, and I can say there were times when I didn't see this ever ending. Through its ups (books 1-6), its downs (8-11), its not-bad-but-could-be-better (7, 12) this has remained a big force in my fantasy reading. Forgive me for this pun, but there will be a <i>void</i> where The Wheel of Time once stood. <br /><br />Favorites died, nations crumbled, deception and betrayal abounded, but fans who flocked to this series for its strengths - the characters, the immense worldbuilding, the complicated plots and plans - will at least be satisfied with Sanderson's strong finale. </span>

</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bdFEjLjw4NhQmw2P2HQZqBEvvv+Hbubf/knCGYY9epm5awJb4y0jw8AeRKtEG0TA94MMjNgpvR1EON0R6y+IxA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GcOxURbjTS2Bha2H7a3FEhiLC/Gr0XOzLRbO0lsalE7NefeGTT6ONhEA5KNxwph6/ie5gvSWKHGXZ9HaNghmEw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan">About Robert Jordan</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1538507642p3/6252.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/6252.Robert_Jordan">Robert Jordan
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
11,435
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15902439300395480219"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br/><br/>Robert Jordan was the pen name of James Oliver Rigney, Jr., under which he was best known as the author of the bestselling The Wheel of Time fantasy series. He also wrote under the names <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/108933.Reagan_O_Neal' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reagan O'Neal</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/943931.Jackson_O_Reilly' title='Jackson O'Reilly' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jackson O'Reilly</a>.<br/><br/>Jordan was born in Charleston, South Carolina. He served two tours in Vietnam (from 1968 to</span>
  <span id="freeText15902439300395480219" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the Goodreads database with this name.</i><br /><br />Robert Jordan was the pen name of James Oliver Rigney, Jr., under which he was best known as the author of the bestselling The Wheel of Time fantasy series. He also wrote under the names <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/108933.Reagan_O_Neal" rel="nofollow noopener">Reagan O'Neal</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/943931.Jackson_O_Reilly" title="Jackson O'Reilly" rel="nofollow noopener">Jackson O'Reilly</a>.<br /><br />Jordan was born in Charleston, South Carolina. He served two tours in Vietnam (from 1968 to 1970) with the United States Army as a helicopter gunner. He was awarded the Distinguished Flying Cross with bronze oak leaf cluster, the Bronze Star with "V" and bronze oak leaf cluster, and two Vietnamese Gallantry Crosses with palm. After returning from Vietnam he attended The Citadel where he received an undergraduate degree in physics. After graduating he was employed by the United States Navy as a nuclear engineer. He began writing in 1977. He was a history buff and enjoyed hunting, fishing, sailing, poker, chess, pool, and pipe collecting. <br /><br />He described himself as a "High Church" Episcopalian and received communion more than once a week. He lived with his wife Harriet McDougal, who works as a book editor (currently with Tor Books; she was also Jordan's editor) in a house built in 1797. <br /><br />Responding to queries on the similarity of some of the concepts in his Wheel of Time books with Freemasonry concepts, Jordan admitted that he was a Freemason. However, "like his father and grandfather," he preferred not to advertise, possibly because of the negative propaganda against Freemasonry. In his own words, "no man in this country should feel in danger because of his beliefs."<br /><br />On March 23, 2006, Jordan disclosed in a statement that he had been diagnosed with cardiac amyloidosis, and that with treatment, his median life expectancy was four years, though he said he intended to beat the statistics. He later posted on his Dragonmount blog to encourage his fans not to worry about him and that he intended to have a long and fully creative life.<br /><br />He began chemotherapy treatment at Mayo Clinic in Rochester, Minnesota, in early April 2006. Jordan was enrolled in a study using the drug Revlimid just approved for multiple myeloma but not yet tested on primary amyloidosis.<br /><br />Jordan died at approximately 2:45 p.m. EDT on September 16, 2007, and a funeral service was held for him on Wednesday, September 19, 2007. Jordan was cremated and his ashes buried in the churchyard of St. James Church in Goose Creek, outside Charleston. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15902439300395480219" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/10558806-a-memory-of-light">Quotes from A Memory of Light</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;He came like the wind, like the wind touched everything, and like the wind was gone.<br /><br />-from The Dragon Reborn. By Loial, son of Arent son of Halan, the Fourth Age.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/703349-he-came-like-the-wind-like-the-wind-touched-everything">192 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Here is your flaw, Shaitan, Lord of the Dark, Lord of Envy, Lord of Nothing, here is why you fail. It was not about me. It’s never been about me.”<br />It was about a woman, torn and beaten down, cast from her throne and made a puppet. A woman who had crawled when she had to. That woman still fought.<br />It was about a man that love repeatedly forsook. A man who found relevance in a world that others would have let pass them by. A man who remembered stories and who took fool boys under his wing when the smarter move would have been to keep on walking. That man still fought.<br />It was about a woman with a secret, a hope for the future. A woman who had hunted the truth before others could. A woman who had given her live, then had it returned. That woman still fought.<br />It was about a man whose family was taken from him, but who stood tall in his sorrow and protected those he could. <br />It was about a woman who refused to believe that she could not help, could not heal those who had been harmed.<br />It was about a hero who insisted with every breath that he was anything but a hero. <br />It was about a woman who would not bend her back while she was beaten, and who shown with a light for all who watched, including Rand.<br />It was about them all.<br />~Rand al Thor&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/702930-here-is-your-flaw-shaitan-lord-of-the-dark-lord">173 likes</a>
            </nobr>

          </div>
